Chapter 66

At the Second Coming, Israel, as a nation, will be born in a day; the wicked will be destroyed; and the Gentiles will hear the gospel.

1 Thus saith the Lord, The heaven is my [athrone](#note1a), and the earth is my footstool: where is the house that ye build unto me? and where is the place of my rest?

2 For all those things hath mine hand made, and all those things have been, saith the Lord: but to this man will I look, even to him that is poor and of a [acontrite spirit](#note2a), and trembleth at my word.

3 [aHe](#note3a) that killeth an ox is as if he slew a man; he that sacrificeth a lamb, as if he cut off a dog’s neck; he that offereth an oblation, as if he offered swine’s blood; he that burneth incense, as if he blessed an idol. Yea, they have chosen their own ways, and their soul delighteth in their abominations.

4 [aI](#note4a) also will choose their delusions, and will bring their fears upon them; because when I [bcalled](#note4b), none did answer; when I spake, they did not hear: but they did evil before mine eyes, and chose that in which I delighted not.

5 ¶ Hear the word of the Lord, ye that tremble at his word; Your brethren that hated you, that [acast](#note5a) you out for my name’s sake, said, Let the Lord be [bglorified](#note5b): but he shall appear to your joy, and they shall be ashamed.

6 A voice of noise from the city, a voice from the temple, a voice of the Lord that rendereth recompence to his enemies.

7 [aBefore](#note7a) she [btravailed](#note7b), she brought forth; before her pain came, she was delivered of a man [cchild](#note7c).

8 Who hath heard such a thing? who hath seen such things? Shall the earth be made to bring forth in one day? or shall a nation be born at once? for as soon as Zion travailed, she brought forth her children.

9 Shall I bring to the birth, and not cause to bring forth? saith the Lord: shall I cause to bring forth, and shut the womb? saith thy God.

10 Rejoice ye with Jerusalem, and be glad with her, all ye that love her: rejoice for joy with her, all ye that mourn for her:

11 That ye may suck, and be satisfied with the breasts of her consolations; that ye may milk out, and be delighted with the abundance of her glory.

12 For thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will extend peace to her [alike a river](#note12a), and the glory of the [bGentiles](#note12b) like a flowing stream: then shall ye suck, ye shall be borne upon her sides, and be dandled upon her knees.

13 As one whom his [amother](#note13a) comforteth, so will I [bcomfort](#note13b) you; and ye shall be [ccomforted](#note13c) in Jerusalem.

14 And when ye see this, your heart shall rejoice, and your bones shall flourish like an herb: and the [ahand](#note14a) of the Lord shall be known toward his servants, and his [bindignation](#note14b) toward his enemies.

15 For, behold, the Lord will come with [afire](#note15a), and with his [bchariots](#note15b) like a whirlwind, to render his anger with fury, and his rebuke with flames of fire.

16 For by fire and by his [asword](#note16a) will [bthe](#note16b) Lord [cplead](#note16c) with all flesh: and the [dslain](#note16d) of the Lord shall be many.

17 They that sanctify themselves, and purify themselves in the gardens behind one tree in the midst, eating swine’s flesh, and the [aabomination](#note17a), and the [bmouse](#note17b), shall be consumed together, saith the Lord.

18 For I [aknow](#note18a) their [bworks](#note18b) and their thoughts: it shall come, that I will gather [call](#note18c) nations and tongues; and they shall come, and see my glory.

19 And I will set a [asign](#note19a) among them, and I will send those that escape of them unto the nations, to Tarshish, Pul, and [bLud](#note19b), that draw the bow, to Tubal, and Javan, to the isles afar off, that have not heard my fame, neither have seen my glory; and they shall [cdeclare](#note19c) my glory among the [dGentiles](#note19d).

20 And they shall bring all your brethren for an [aoffering](#note20a) unto the Lord out of all nations upon horses, and in chariots, and in litters, and upon mules, and upon swift beasts, to my holy mountain Jerusalem, saith the Lord, as the children of Israel bring an offering in a clean vessel into the house of the Lord.

21 And I will also take of them for [apriests](#note21a) and for Levites, saith the Lord.

22 For as the [anew](#note22a) heavens and the new earth, which I will make, shall remain before me, saith the Lord, so shall your [bseed](#note22b) and your name remain.

23 And it shall come to pass, that from one new moon to another, and from one sabbath to another, shall all flesh come to [aworship](#note23a) before me, saith the Lord.

24 And they shall go forth, and look upon the carcases of the men that have transgressed against me: for their [aworm](#note24a) shall not die, neither shall their [bfire](#note24b) be quenched; and they shall be an abhorring unto all flesh.
